msg:Our experience at this hotel was a complete nightmare and marred what was otherwise an incredible trip through China. From the moment we arrived, we were met with indifference and incompetence. Despite explicitly asking for English-speaking staff, we were left to fend for ourselves with no assistance whatsoever.

The room itself was a horror show; it was disgustingly dirty, with filth and grime in every corner. Dust coated the bathroom sink, and there were even hairs in the toilet. It was utterly revolting.

But what truly made our blood boil was the hotel's complete disregard for basic services. Despite arranging for parcel deliveries beforehand, they rejected them upon arrival, causing us endless headaches. And don't even get me started on the lack of room service ‚Äì having to trudge down to the lobby for a simple cup of coffee felt like a slap in the face.

To add insult to injury, the promised welcome gift was nowhere to be found. It was yet another disappointment in a string of failures at this hotel. Not only did they fail to deliver on basic cleanliness and services, but they also neglected to provide the simple gesture of a welcome gift, as promised. It was the cherry on top of an already disastrous experience, leaving us feeling completely disheartened and betrayed. This was the only bad hotel experience we had during our entire trip through China, and it stuck out like a sore thumb compared to the other five hotels we stayed at. It's a shame that such incompetence can overshadow what should have been a memorable journey.

msg:I recently had the pleasure of staying at UrCove by Hyatt Foshan, and it was an outstanding experience.

The hotel was perfect in every way and exceptionally clean. From the moment I arrived, I was impressed by the spotless environment and the attention to detail in maintaining high standards of cleanliness throughout the hotel.

The location is excellent and convenient for any traveler. The hotel is attached to a mall featuring high-end brands and well-known shops, making shopping effortless. Whether you need to pick up some essentials or indulge in a bit of retail therapy, everything is just a short walk away.

Food options are abundant and easily accessible. There are numerous restaurants and eateries nearby, offering a variety of cuisines to suit any palate.

In summary, UrCove by Hyatt Foshan is a fantastic choice for anyone visiting the area. The impeccable cleanliness, prime location, and proximity to shopping and dining options make it highly recommendable for your trip.

5. There is no Bluetooth speaker. The smart guest control machine cannot be moved at will, and the sound quality is average.
6. The Yifei smart butler cannot be turned on, and the customer service can only be called.

In general, the price is more cost-effective and the experience is acceptable.

1. The hotel check-in policy states that check-in is at 2 o'clock. We arrived at the hotel at 2:40. The front desk told us that the room was fully booked the day before and it would take another 40 minutes. May I ask if the new customer should be responsible for the late check-out of the previous day and the cleaning is not done? If you can't check in at 2 o'clock, why can't the check-in policy be changed to 3 o'clock or 4 o'clock?
2. Wait until 3:30 and ask the front desk again. I was still told that the room was still being checked. Finally, I successfully got the room card at about 4 o'clock.
3. The sound insulation of the room is very poor. There is a bar street nearby, and it is still noisy after 23 o'clock. People with light sleep should choose carefully.
4. The most basic Wi-Fi is terrible. The Wi-Fi is very slow. It "strikes" directly at night and can't connect to the Internet. I called the front desk and the front desk said, "Our Wi-Fi can't be used either. You can use your own data first." May I ask if your hotel Wi-Fi doesn't work, don't you contact the staff immediately to troubleshoot the problem? They also said "our employees can't use it either". Do they need customers to empathize with them?
5. The room layout is unreasonable. We booked an executive city view room. There was only a table with a chair in the room. There was not even a coffee table in front of the sofa. What's even funnier is that there was a bathtub next to the sofa. It was far away from the shower room and you had to cross the whole bed. There was also the sound of running water at night...
